| 0:52:19| you record things just like a for-profit company would.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267150126?start=3139)|

| 0:52:31| other than the fact that there should have been, well, there was a difference.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267150126?start=3151)|
| 0:52:36| The funding has to be done from the county to the schools.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267150126?start=3156)|
| 0:52:40| In other words, the schools cannot incur debt.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267150126?start=3160)|
